!Charlie Briegel, X4510, FNAL
!Allen-Bradley SLC 504 is connected via DH+ from a VME Crate
!	The data to be data pooled can be specified by the startup script.  An
! oid is mapped to a single SLC 504 specified again by the startup script.
!       Reading supports three data types, ADC, Binary Status, and ASCII name
! of the SLC 504 connected to the specified OID and FE.  The ADC has an
! explicit offset in the code and starts at N7:140.
!	Currently, there is support for setting, but no instances of such
! devices.
!	Basic status supports individual bits as 1 or 0 and are alarmable.
!	Basic control allows on/off/reset for the four supplies; lower, quad,
! upper, and house.
!	The convention for names is for testing purposes, specified before
! I realized there was a standard, and totally modifiable. 
!
!................DABBEL entries begin.............................................
! 
!****************** Devices for MI60N *********************
!
! Examples of PS building devices
!
 MOD I:PS6NAD ( 'MI60N ADC devices' , MI60N ,          , 7FFFFFE )
!	Naming convention..................................................
!x:PSyyxx   	x: subsystem aligned with devices, i.e. I=MI or J=Prelim MI
!		PS = power supply system
!		yy = building number
!		xx = data type
!		AD=analog, NM=name, LW=lower, UP=upper, QD=quad, HS=house
!		ST=status, SL=status lower, SQ=status quad, SU=status upper, 
!		SH=status house
 SSDNHX READNG (0A30/0090/0000/2700)
!               |||| |||| |||| ||-->>>>channel
!               |||| |||| |||| -->>>>class (allen-bradley=0x27)
!               |||| |||| ---->>>>misc type = ADC(0),binary status(1),name(2)
!		|||| ---->>oid (allen-bradley=0x90; MI60 (0x91, 0x92))
!               ||-->>>>node (MI60N)
!               -->>>>trunk
! Able to read 4 chans of AI with nominal 1X scaling factor to volts
 PRO READNG ( 2 ,     8 ,    120 )
 PDB READNG ( 'Volt' , 'Volt' , 10 ,  2 , 2 , 0 , 0 , 0 , 1.0 , 2560. , 0.0)
 PRO SAVE (4,0707,0700,ALL)		!Generic Green device
!          |  | |  Generic Device (Powered Down to be Green (save Energy))
!          |  | Exclude the following
!          |  Basic Status(bit2), Setting(bit1), Reading(bit0)
!          Special List
!
 MOD I:PS6NST ( 'MI60N PS Status' , MI60N ,          , 7FFFFFE )
 SSDNHX READNG (0A30/0090/0001/2700)
!               |||| |||| |||| ||-->>>>channel
!               |||| |||| |||| -->>>>class (allen-bradley=0x27)
!               |||| |||| ---->>>>misc type = ADC(0),binary status(1),vers(2)
!		|||| ---->>oid (allen-bradley=0x90; MI60 (0x91, 0x92))
!               ||-->>>>node (MI60N)
!               -->>>>trunk
! 3*4*16 bits of Digital Status, only 24 bytes currently retrieved
 PRO READNG ( 2 ,     24 ,    120 )
 PDB READNG ( 'Stat' , 'Stat' , 10 ,  0 , 2 , 0 , 0 , 0 , 0 , 0 , 0)
 PRO SAVE (4,0707,0700,ALL)		!Generic Green device
!
 MOD I:PS6NNM ( 'MI60N Allen-Bradley Name' , MI60N ,          , 7FFFFFE )
 SSDNHX READNG (0A30/0090/0002/2700)
 PRO READNG ( 4 ,     8 ,    120 )
 PDB READNG ( 'Text' , 'Text' , 10 ,  0 , 4 , 0 , 1 , 0 , 0 , 0 , 0)
 PRO SAVE (4,0707,0700,ALL)		!GPIB Generic Green device
!
! Examples of PS individual devices
!
 MOD I:L6N+5 ( 'MI60N Lambda Supply +5' , MI60N ,          , 7FFFFFE )
!	Naming convention..................................................
!x:abcdef   	x: subsystem aligned with devices, i.e. I=MI or J=Prelim MI
!		abcdef = arbitrary 
 SSDNHX READNG (0A30/0090/0000/2700)
 PRO READNG ( 2 ,     2 ,    120 )
 PDB READNG ( 'Volt' , 'Volt' , 10 ,  2 , 2 , 0 , 0 , 0 , 1.0 , 2560. , 0.0)
